## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population size P. Classical population dynamics provides numerous ODE models relating growth rate to current population, ranging from simple exponential growth to complex models with Allee effects, seasonal forcing, and density-dependent mechanisms.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, no density dependence)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / (P + c2)) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth, common in tumor/population modeling)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with flexible inflection point)
- Logistic with Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below critical threshold)
- Logistic with Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (reduced per-capita growth at low density)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism vs catabolism balance)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized asymmetric growth curve)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (logistic with periodic environmental forcing)
- Exponential with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**c2 (growth with density-dependent removal)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional power density dependence)
- Logistic with time-varying rate: dP_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) * P * (1 - c2 * P) (changing intrinsic growth rate)
- Beverton-Holt continuous analog: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (saturating reproduction minus mortality)
- Cubic population model: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (polynomial density dependence with multiple equilibria)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Proportionality to P ŌåÆ conservation of per-capita biological processes (each individual contributes to growth): dP_dt contains factor of P
- Quadratic P terms (P*(1-cP) or P^2) ŌåÆ pairwise interactions/competition for resources among individuals
- Cubic P terms or triple products ŌåÆ Allee effects or multiple stable equilibria in population dynamics
- Logarithmic dependence on P (log(K/P)) ŌåÆ multiplicative rather than additive approach to carrying capacity (Gompertz-type)
- Trigonometric functions of t ŌåÆ seasonal or periodic environmental forcing on population dynamics
- Ratio P/(1+cP) ŌåÆ saturating functional response (Holling Type II) limiting per-capita resource intake
- Product of multiple linear factors in P ŌåÆ multiple critical population thresholds (extinction, carrying capacity)
- Exponential dependence on t without P ŌåÆ externally driven environmental change independent of population feedback
- Fractional powers of P (P^c where 0<c<1) ŌåÆ surface-area-to-volume scaling in metabolic/growth models
- Negative constant term independent of P ŌåÆ constant-yield harvesting or immigration effects

Candidate formulas: 50

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine if any candidate can match it.

**Step 1: Simplify the GT expression.**

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.17*(P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 - P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 - exp(-0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand this. Let me use exact coefficients: a = 0.1699888, b = 1/1.047284 Ōēł 0.9549, d = 1/10.2105 Ōēł 0.09794, k = 0.09709.

**Term 1:** `a*(P*b - 1)*(1 - d*P)*P = a*(bP - 1)*(1 - dP)*P`
= a*P*(bP - 1 - bdP┬▓ + dP) = a*(-bdP┬│ + (b+d)P┬▓ - P)

**Term 2:** `a*(1 - d*P)*P = a*(P - dP┬▓)`

**Term 3:** `a*(1 - exp(-kP))*P = a*(P - P*exp(-kP))`

Combining Terms 1+2+3:
- P┬│ term: `-a*b*d*P┬│`
- P┬▓ term: `a*(b+d)*P┬▓ - a*d*P┬▓` = `a*b*P┬▓`
- P term: `-a*P + a*P + a*P` = `a*P`
- Exponential term: `-a*P*exp(-kP)`

So GT = `-a*b*d*P┬│ + a*b*P┬▓ + a*P - a*P*exp(-kP)`

Numerically: GT Ōēł `-0.01589*P┬│ + 0.1623*P┬▓ + 0.17*P - 0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)`

**Step 2: Check candidates with exponential terms.**

The GT has a `P*exp(-kP)` term, so I need candidates with exponential terms in P.

**Candidate 50:** `P┬│*c0 + P┬▓*c1 + c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`
This has `exp(c3*P)` but GT needs `P*exp(-kP)`. Not equivalent.

**Candidate 49:** `P┬│*c0 + P┬▓*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`
GT = `-0.01589*P┬│ + 0.1623*P┬▓ + 0.17*P - 0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)`
= `c0*P┬│ + c1*P┬▓ + c2*P*exp(c3*P) + c4`

Setting: c0 = -0.01589, c1 = 0.1623, c2 = -0.17, c3 = -0.097, c4 = 0.17*P...

Wait, the remaining term is `0.17*P`, but candidate 49 has no standalone `P` term. We have `c4` as a constant, not `P`. So this doesn't work unless... no, we need a linear P term.

**Candidate 33:** `P┬│*c0/(P*c1 + c2) + P┬▓*c3/(P*c1 + c2) + P*c4/(P*c1 + c2) + P*c5 + c6`
If c1=0, this becomes `P┬│*c0/c2 + P┬▓*c3/c2 + P*c4/c2 + P*c5 + c6`, which is a polynomial. Can't produce exponential.

**Candidate 17:** `P┬│*c0/(P*c1 + c2) + P┬▓*c3/(P*c1 + c2) + c4 + c5*exp(P*c6 + c7*t)`
This has `exp(c6*P + c7*t)`. Setting c7=0: `c5*exp(c6*P)`. But GT needs `P*exp(-kP)`, not just `exp`. No match.

**Candidate 45:** `P┬│*c0 + P┬▓*c1 + c2 + c3*log(c4*exp(P*c5) + 1)`
For large negative c5*P, log(1) ŌåÆ 0. For large positive, log Ōēł c5*P. This is log-based, not matching.

None of the candidates contain a `P*exp(cP)` term alongside polynomial terms `P┬│, P┬▓, P` (4 terms needed). Candidate 49 is closest but lacks a standalone `P` term.

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG9)

GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - P/c7)*P + c8*(c9 - exp(-c10*P))*P
Candidates evaluated: 50

Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine which candidates can match it.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.17*(ŌłÆ1 + P/1.047)*(1 ŌłÆ P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 ŌłÆ P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 ŌłÆ exp(ŌłÆ0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand this. Let me use exact coefficients for clarity.

**Term 1:** `0.17*(-1 + P/1.047)*(1 - P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*(P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21)*P

**Term 2:** `0.17*(1 - P/10.21)*P`
= 0.17*P - 0.17*P┬▓/10.21

**Term 3:** `0.17*(1 - exp(-0.097*P))*P`
= 0.17*P - 0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)

Let me expand Term 1:
(P/1.047 - 1)*(1 - P/10.21) = P/1.047 - P┬▓/(1.047*10.21) - 1 + P/10.21

So Term 1 = 0.17*P*[P/1.047 - P┬▓/(1.047*10.21) - 1 + P/10.21]
= 0.17*[P┬▓/1.047 - P┬│/(1.047*10.21) - P + P┬▓/10.21]

Combining all three terms:
- **P┬│ term:** -0.17/(1.047*10.21) * P┬│
- **P┬▓ terms:** 0.17/1.047 * P┬▓ + 0.17/10.21 * P┬▓ - 0.17/10.21 * P┬▓  = 0.17/1.047 * P┬▓
- **P terms:** -0.17*P + 0.17*P + 0.17*P = 0.17*P
- **Exponential term:** -0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)

So GT = **-0.17/(1.047*10.21) * P┬│ + 0.17/1.047 * P┬▓ + 0.17*P - 0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)**

Let me compute constants:
- P┬│ coefficient: -0.17/(10.69) Ōēł -0.0159
- P┬▓ coefficient: 0.17/1.047 Ōēł 0.1623
- P coefficient: 0.17
- Exp term: -0.17*P*exp(-0.097*P)

So GT = a*P┬│ + b*P┬▓ + c*P + d*P*exp(e*P)

where a Ōēł -0.0159, b Ōēł 0.1623, c Ōēł 0.17, d Ōēł -0.17, e Ōēł -0.097.

The GT contains **four basis function types**: P┬│, P┬▓, P, and P*exp(╬▒P).

This is crucial: the GT has a **P*exp(╬▒P)** term. Any candidate that lacks an exponential term cannot match unless the exponential can somehow be absorbed, which is impossible due to linear independence of polynomial and exponential functions.

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidates without exponentials or logs (purely rational/polynomial):
Candidates 1-8, 10-16, 19-27, 29-36, 38-40, 43-44, 47-48: These are rational functions or polynomials. They cannot produce a P*exp(╬▒P) term. **[NO MATCH]** for all of these.

### Candidate 9: `P┬│c0/(Pc1+c2) + P┬▓c3/(Pc1+c2) + c4*exp(P*c5) + c6`
This has exp(P*c5) but GT needs P*exp(╬▒P). These are linearly independent. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 17: `P┬│c0/(Pc1+c2) + P┬▓c3/(Pc1+c2) + c4 + c5*exp(Pc6 + c7*t)`
Has t-dependence (can set c7=0), giving exp(Pc6), not P*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 18: `P┬│c0/(Pc1+c2) + P┬▓c3/(Pc1+c2) + c4*exp(P*c5)`
Same issue - exp(Pc5) ŌēĀ P*exp(╬▒P). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 28: `P┬│c0/(Pc1+c2) + P┬▓c3 + c4*exp(P┬▓c5)` - wrong exp argument. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 37, 41, 42, 45, 46: These have log terms. log ŌēĀ P*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 49: `P┬│c0 + P┬▓c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`
This has P*exp(Pc3)! GT = a*P┬│ + b*P┬▓ + c*P + d*P*exp(eP). Setting c4=c (absorbing the linear P term into... wait, there's no standalone P term here). We need a P term but candidate 49 doesn't have one. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 50: `P┬│c0 + P┬▓c1 + c2*exp(P*c3) + c4`
Missing P term and has exp not P*exp. **[NO MATCH]**

Matched candidate IDs: []
